style="display:flex;flex-direction:row;justify-content:space-between"><h1 id="shipping-module" class="dx-anchor dx-content-title newArchetype"> <span id="#shipping-module" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#shipping-module" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Shipping module</h1></div><div class="badgesRow"><style data-emotion="css jaf4zm-badge_base-text_caption-feature">.css-jaf4zm-badge_base-text_caption-feature{color:#001435;font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,"Helvetica Neue",Arial,sans-serif;font-size:0.875rem;line-height:1.25rem;font-weight:400;max-width:18rem;overflow:hidden;word-break:break-word;text-transform:none;-webkit-line-clamp:2;display:-webkit-inline-box;-webkit-box-orient:vertical;height:auto;padding:0.125rem 0.5rem;border-radius:0.5rem;color:#ffffff;background-color:#7252cc;}@media screen and (max-width: 752px){.css-jaf4zm-badge_base-text_caption-feature{font-size:min(0.875rem, 28px);line-height:min(1.25rem, 40px);}}[dir='rtl'] .css-jaf4zm-badge_base-text_caption-feature{text-align:right;}</style><span class="css-jaf4zm-badge_base-text_caption-feature" data-ppui-info="badge_3.4.10__7.46.3" style="margin-right:8px">Current</span><p class="lastUpdated">Last updated: <!-- -->Jul 7th, 4:35am</p></div></div></div></div><div style="background:white" class="navigationWrapper"><div class="navigationWrapper css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"></div></div></div></div><div><div id="overview" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="overview" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#overview" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#overview" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Overview</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>The shipping module presents shipping details to a buyer during the Pay with PayPal and Pay with Venmo flow. The merchant has several options available for controlling how shipping addresses and shipping options are handled. The server-side shipping callbacks allow
    you to update the shipping and order amount information as buyers make changes on the review page.</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="merchant-and-buyer-interaction" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#merchant-and-buyer-interaction" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#merchant-and-buyer-interaction" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Merchant and buyer interaction</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Buyers can use the shipping module to specify the shipping address and shipping options on the review page. The system sends a callback to the merchant's URL with the updated shipping information.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>When the buyer provides their shipping address, a callback is sent to the merchant server with the buyer's address using the server-side shipping callbacks. In response, the merchant can send the shipping options and updated order
    cost amounts.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>You can use server-side callbacks to:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>Verify that you support the shipping method.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Update shipping costs.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Change line items in the cart.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Inform the buyer that you do not support their shipping method.</span></li><span>
</span></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--info__ZzK8d"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><style data-emotion="css 4757ty-svg-size_xs">.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs{speak:none;display:inline-block;aspect-ratio:1;width:1.125rem;height:1.125rem;}.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs img,.css-4757ty-svg-size_xs svg{width:100%;height:100%;display:block;}</style><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="info" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>While both server-side and client-side callbacks are possible, it is generally recommended to use server-side callbacks, as client-side callbacks may not be available in all situations.&nbsp;For example, client-side callbacks using JS-SDK are designed primarily for web-based integrations and are incompatible with Venmo. They may not be suitable for native mobile applications that often require different APIs or SDKs tailored for mobile platforms.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>The following sample PayPal and Venmo&nbsp;review pages show a buyer's shipping address and options:</span></p><span>
</span><p><span> </span><img filename="undefined" src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/ShipModPWVReviewUpdates.png" ecmid="undefined" alt="image" width="715" style="object-fit:contain;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto" id="image" title="undefined" height="715"/><span> </span></p><span>


</span><div style="display:flex;justify-content:center;align-items:center;gap:20px"><span>
    </span><div><br/></div><span>
    </span><div><br/></div><span>
</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="how-it-works" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="how-it-works" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#how-it-works" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#how-it-works" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->How it works</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>The shipping address and options callback process involves the following steps:</span></p><span>


</span><p><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>A buyer clicks on the PayPal&nbsp;or Venmo button displayed on the merchant site.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The merchant makes a&nbsp;Create Order API request to set up the flow, including the parameters needed to enable the server-side callbacks.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The buyer is taken to the flow where they are authenticated and shown the review page.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>A server-side callback is created to the merchant's server with the default shipping address from the buyer's wallet.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The merchant processes the callback and responds with shipping options for the address and updated order amount.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The review page updates to reflect the merchant's revised order amount and shipping options.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>If the buyer changes the shipping address or shipping options, a callback is made to the merchant. The merchant's response updates the review page.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The buyer clicks the pay button on the review page to complete the transaction, which is returned to the merchant.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The merchant may make a Show Order Details API call to get the final&nbsp;order information and verify it still matches the information in their system.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The merchant captures the&nbsp;order to complete the transaction.</span></li><span>
</span></ol></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="create-order" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="create-order" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#create-order" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#create-order" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Create order</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Use the Orders v2 API </span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/studio/checkout/standard/integrate#create-order" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Create Order</span></a><span> request to set up the flow used by the buyer to approve a transaction. Both Pay with PayPal and Pay with Venmo support the shipping module.&nbsp;The request can utilize either </span><code class=""><span>payment_source:paypal</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>payment_source:venmo</span></code><span>. There are several
    ways to determine how the shipping address and options are displayed on the review page and which events create callbacks when the buyer interacts with them.</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3>Enabling server-side callbacks</h3><span>
</span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>payment_source.*.experience_context.order_update_callback_config</span></code><span> object is used to enable and configure server-side callbacks during the flow. The </span><code class=""><span>callback_url</span></code><span> field specifies the endpoint on your
    servers where the&nbsp;callback request is sent. The </span><code class=""><span>callback_events</span></code><span> array specifies which callback events you support. The flow supports the following events:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>SHIPPING_ADDRESS</span></code><span>: This event happens when the review page loads for the first time and when the buyer changes their shipping address. We recommend merchants to subscribe only to </span><code class=""><span>SHIPPING_ADDRESS</span></code><span>. This
        requires a merchant to respond with all the shipping options and amounts calculated on the initial callback. Since all options have been returned, the merchant callback does not have to be called when the selection option changes. This method
        reduces delays and the number of requests.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>SHIPPING_OPTIONS</span></code><span>: This event happens when the buyer selects new shipping options and when they change shipping options. We recommend merchants subscribe to this if they want to be notified or need to recalculate amounts with
        their callback URL when a selected shipping option changes for the current address. If </span><code class=""><span>SHIPPING_OPTIONS</span></code><span> is not needed by the merchant, they should subscribe to </span><code class=""><span>SHIPPING_ADDRESS</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3>Configuring shipping preferences</h3><span>
</span><p><span>The shipping preference is set using the </span><code class=""><span>payment_source.*.experience_context.shipping_preference</span></code><span> field. There are 3 possible values:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>GET_FROM_FILE</span></code><span>: This default preference retrieves the customer-provided shipping address from their wallet.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>NO_SHIPPING</span></code><span>: This option removes the shipping address information from the review page and the API response. However, the </span><code class=""><span>shipping.phone_number</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>shipping.email_address</span></code><span> fields are returned
        for digital goods delivery.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>SET_PROVIDED_ADDRESS</span></code><span>: The review page shows the shipping address provided by the merchant in the create order request. The buyer cannot change this address on the review page. If the merchant does not pass an address, the
        buyer can choose the address on the review page.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p><span>If you do not pass a shipping preference, the default behavior is </span><code class=""><span>GET_FROM_FILE</span></code><span>. The review page shows the default shipping address from the buyer's wallet. The buyer can select a different shipping address from
    their wallet or add a new address. Callbacks happen if the shipping preference is </span><code class=""><span>GET_FROM_FILE</span></code><span>.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h3 id="pass-shipping-address" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#pass-shipping-address" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#pass-shipping-address" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Passing a shipping address</h3><span>
</span><p><span>If you have a shipping address from the buyer, pass it to Pay with PayPal or Pay with Venmo&nbsp;on the create order request. If you pass a shipping address with a shipping preference of </span><code class=""><span>GET_FROM_FILE</span></code><span>, it will display on the review page, where the buyer can change the shipping address. You can use the shipping preference </span><code class=""><span>SET_PROVIDED_ADDRESS</span></code><span> to prevent the buyer from changing the shipping address on the review page. </span><br/><span>If your transaction does not involve shipping, you can pass the shipping preference </span><code class=""><span>NO_SHIPPING</span></code><span>&nbsp;and no shipping information will be displayed on the review page.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Here is a sample Create Order API request to a merchant with a callback config for Pay with PayPal (</span><code class=""><span>payment_source:paypal</span></code><span>) and Pay with Venmo (</span><code class=""><span>payment_source:venmo</span></code><span>).</span></p></div><div class="codeBlockComponent"><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div id="server-side-shipping-callbacks" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="server-side-shipping-callbacks" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#server-side-shipping-callbacks" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#server-side-shipping-callbacks" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Server-side shipping callbacks</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>The Server-Side Callback API request to a merchant is consistent with GET orders and includes selected addresses and options outside of the order object.</span></p><p></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>Sending order data is structurally similar to making a GET request.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Updated shipping addresses and options separately sent from the order to avoid confusion.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>If the address or option is incomplete, it will not be set in order to prevent misunderstandings.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>The cart identifier will be embedded in the callback URL if merchants cannot associate their shopping cart with the order.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Merchants with client-side shopping carts should include item details when they create the order for server-side shipping callbacks.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="callback-request-for-shipping-address-event" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#callback-request-for-shipping-address-event" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#callback-request-for-shipping-address-event" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Callback request to merchant for shipping address event</h3><span>
</span><p><span>The following sample is a server-side callback request to the merchant for a shipping event. The callback identifies the order, </span><code class=""><span>shipping_address</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>shipping_option</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>purchase_units</span></code><span>.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--warning__0usR0"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span         </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>purchase_units</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Defines the purchase unit. Includes </span><code class=""><span>reference_id</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>amount</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>object</span></p>
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>reference_id</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Identifier associated with the purchase units. For example, </span><code class=""><span>d9f80740-38f0-11e8-b467-0ed5f89f718b</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>string</span></p>
            </td>
        </tr>



    </tbody>
</table></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="merchant-response" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><h2 id="merchant-response" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#merchant-response" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#merchant-response" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Merchant response</h2></div><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>The merchant response to a server-side callback request is similar to an order. A change to the customers shipping address or options can affect the following fields within the data structure:</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>purchase_units[].shipping.options</span></code><span> represent the shipping modules associated with the purchase units within the order. The purchase order field includes contact and delivery information, including phone
        number,&nbsp;account email address, order ID, and reference ID.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><code class=""><span>purchase_units[].amount</span></code><span> represents the purchase unit amount in the order.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>

</span><p><span>Buyer changes can be managed through&nbsp;one of the following approaches:</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>Asking the merchant to return an updated order limited to the fields that can be changed.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Asking the merchant to return a list of patch operations.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="merchant-success-response" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#merchant-success-response" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#merchant-success-response" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Merchant success response</h3><span>
</span><p><span>When the order request is acceptable, the merchant responds with a success message that contains amount and shipping option changes.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Here is a sample HTTP </span><code class=""><span>200 OK</span></code><span> callback response from a merchant with shipping options and amount updates.</span></p></div><div data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h3 id="merchant-success-response-fields" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#merchant-success-response-fields" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#merchant-success-response-fields" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Merchant success response fields</h3><span>
</span><p><span>A merchant response can include the fields identified in the following table.</span></p><span>
</span><table data-ppui-info="table_3.22.1__7.46.3" class="ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">
    <tbody class="css-1da1jgi-tbody" data-ppui="true">
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <th><span>
                </span><p><strong><span>Field</span></strong></p><span>
            </span></th>
            <th><span>
                </span><p><strong><span>Description</span></strong></p><span>
            </span></th>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><strong><span>Date type</span></strong></td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>id</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Identifies the merchant. For example, </span><code class=""><span>8HFTASDATTV</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">string</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>purchase_units</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Purchase unit information. Includes </span><code class=""><span>reference_id</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>amount</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>reference_id</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Uniquely identifies the purchase transaction. For example, </span><code class=""><span>d9f80740-38f0-11e8-b467-0ed5f89f718b</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">string</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>amount</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Purchase unit amount in the order. Includes </span><code class=""><span>currency_code</span></code><span>,</span><code class=""><span>value</span></code><span>, and </span><code class=""><span>breakdown</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>currency_code</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Code indicating the amount currency type. For example, </span><code class=""><span>USD</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">string</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>value</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>String denoting the purchase unit amount in the order, formatted as </span><code class=""><span>X.XX</span></code><span>. For example, </span><code class=""><span>105.00</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">amount</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>breakdown</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Amount breakdown. Includes </span><code class=""><span>item_total</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>tax_total,</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>shipping</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>item_total</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Amount item breakdown. Includes </span><code class=""><span>currency_code</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>value</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
        </tr>

        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">

            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Amount item value. For example, </span><code class=""><span>100.0</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">number</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>tax_total</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Amount tax breakdown. Includes </span><code class=""><span>currency_code</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>value</span></code><span>.&nbsp;</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
        </tr>

        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>value</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>String denoting the</span><code class=""><span>tax_total</span></code><span> amount, formatted as </span><code class=""><span>X.XX</span></code><span>. For example, </span><code class=""><span>5.00</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">number</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>shipping</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Amount shipping breakdown. Includes </span><code class=""><span>currency_code</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>value</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
        </tr>

        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>value</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>String denoting the value. amount, formatted as </span><code class=""><span>X.XX</span></code><span>. For example, </span><code class=""><span>0.00</span></code><span>. </span></p>
                <p><span>In this example, there are no shipping costs associated with the purchase unit.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">number</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>shipping_options</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Shipping option information. Includes </span><code class=""><span>id</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>amount</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>type</span></code><span>, </span><code class=""><span>label</span></code><span>, and </span><code class=""><span>selected</span></code><span>. </span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>selected</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">Determines which options are selected by default. Possible values are <code class=""><span>true</span></code> or <code class=""><span>false</span></code>.</td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">boolean</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>id</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Shipping option identifier. For example, </span><code class=""><span>1</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">number</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>amount</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Amount for the selected shipping option. For example,&nbsp;</span><code class=""><span>currency_code</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>value</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
        </tr>

        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>value</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>String denoting the value. amount for the selected shipping option, formatted as </span><code class=""><span>X.XX</span></code><span>. For example, </span><code class=""><span>0.00</span></code><span>. The value depends upon the selected </span><code class=""><span>label</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">number</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>type</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>An enum that indicates the type of delivery for the selected option. For example,&nbsp;</span><code class=""><span>SHIPPING</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>PICKUP</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">string</td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>label</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Dropdown menu option selected by the buyer. Indicates the type of </span><code class=""><span>SHIPPING</span></code><span>. For example, </span><code class=""><span>Free Shipping</span></code><span>. </span><br/><span>Other labels include </span><code class=""><span>USPS Priority Shipping</span></code><span> and </span><code class=""><span>1-Day Shipping</span></code><span>.</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">string</td>
        </tr>

    </tbody>
</table><span>
</span><p><span>The order amount automatically updates based on the options selected by buyers unless you are subscribed to the </span><code class=""><span>shipping_options</span></code><span> callback. If you are subscribed to </span><code class=""><span>shipping_options</span></code><span>, ensure the callback response includes the updated total cost so that the checkout page can be updated.&nbsp;You can use the </span><code class=""><span>onShippingOptionsChange()</span></code><span> callback to update your own database with the new cost amount.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h3 id="merchant-decline-response" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#merchant-decline-response" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#merchant-decline-response" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Merchant decline response</h3><span>
</span><p><span>A merchant can issue a </span><code class=""><span>422</span></code><span> error to decline a callback event.&nbsp;In the response, the merchant should provide a reason why the callback is being declined. The following reasons are supported:</span></p><span>

</span><table data-ppui-info="table_3.22.1__7.46.3" class="ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">
    <tbody class="css-1da1jgi-tbody" data-ppui="true">
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <th><span>
                </span><p><span>Callback event type</span></p><span>
            </span></th>
            <th><span>
                </span><p><span>Error</span></p><span>
            </span></th>
            <th><span>
                </span><p><span>Description</span></p><span>
            </span></th>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Shipping address</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>ADDRESS_ERROR</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Your order can't be shipped to this address.</span></p>
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Shipping address</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>COUNTRY_ERROR</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Your order can't be shipped to this country.</span></p>
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Shipping address</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>STATE_ERROR</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Your order can't be shipped to this state.</span></p>
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Shipping address</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>ZIP_ERROR</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Your order can't be shipped to this zip.</span></p>
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Shipping option</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>METHOD_UNAVAILABLE</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>The shipping method you selected is unavailable. To continue, choose another way to get your order.</span></p>
            </td>
        </tr>
        <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Shipping option</span></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><code class=""><span>STORE_UNAVAILABLE</span></code></p>
            </td>
            <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">
                <p><span>Part of your order isn't available at this store.</span></p>
            </td>
        </tr>
    </tbody>
</table><span>

</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><p><span>Here is a sample decline callback from the merchant. The merchant has several options available for controlling how shipping addresses and shipping options are handled. The server-side shipping callbacks allow\n    you to update the shipping and order amount information as buyers make changes on the review page.\n\n \n\n### Merchant and buyer interaction\nBuyers can use the shipping module to specify the shipping address and shipping options on the review page. The system sends a callback to the merchant's URL with the updated shipping information.\n\nWhen the buyer provides their shipping address, a callback is sent to the merchant server with the buyer's address using the server-side shipping callbacks. In response, the merchant can send the shipping options and updated order\n    cost amounts.\n\nYou can use server-side callbacks to:\n\n- Verify that you support the shipping method.\n- Update shipping costs.\n- Change line items in the cart.\n- Inform the buyer that you do not support their shipping method.\n\n\n**info**\nWhile both server-side and client-side callbacks are possible, it is generally recommended to use server-side callbacks, as client-side callbacks may not be available in all situations.For example, client-side callbacks using JS-SDK are designed primarily for web-based integrations and are incompatible with Venmo. They may not be suitable for native mobile applications that often require different APIs or SDKs tailored for mobile platforms.\n\n\nThe following sample PayPal and Venmoreview pages show a buyer's shipping address and options:\n\n ![image](https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/ShipModPWVReviewUpdates.png) \n\n  \n\n## How it works \nThe shipping address and options callback process involves the following steps:\n\n\n\n- A buyer clicks on the PayPalor Venmo button displayed on the merchant site.\n- The merchant makes aCreate Order API request to set up the flow, including the parameters needed to enable the server-side callbacks.\n- The buyer is taken to the flow where they are authenticated and shown the review page.\n- A server-side callback is created to the merchant's server with the default shipping address from the buyer's wallet.\n- The merchant processes the callback and responds with shipping options for the address and updated order amount.\n- The review page updates to reflect the merchant's revised order amount and shipping options.\n- If the buyer changes the shipping address or shipping options, a callback is made to the merchant. The merchant's response updates the review page.\n- The buyer clicks the pay button on the review page to complete the transaction, which is returned to the merchant.\n- The merchant may make a Show Order Details API call to get the finalorder information and verify it still matches the information in their system.\n- The merchant captures theorder to complete the transaction.\n\n\n\n## Create order \nUse the Orders v2 API [Create Order](https://developer.paypal.com/studio/checkout/standard/integrate#create-order) request to set up the flow used by the buyer to approve a transaction. Both Pay with PayPal and Pay with Venmo support the shipping module.The request can utilize either payment_source:paypal or payment_source:venmo . There are several\n    ways to determine how the shipping address and options are displayed on the review page and which events create callbacks when the buyer interacts with them.\n\n \n\n### Enabling server-side callbacks\nThe payment_source.*.experience_context.order_update_callback_config object is used to enable and configure server-side callbacks during the flow. The callback_url field specifies the endpoint on your\n    servers where thecallback request is sent. The callback_events array specifies which callback events you support. The flow supports the following events:\n\n- SHIPPING_ADDRESS : This event happens when the review page loads for the first time and when the buyer changes their shipping address. We recommend merchants to subscribe only to SHIPPING_ADDRESS . This\n        requires a merchant to respond with all the shipping options and amounts calculated on the initial callback. Since all options have been returned, the merchant callback does not have to be called when the selection option changes. This method\n        reduces delays and the number of requests.\n\n- SHIPPING_OPTIONS : This event happens when the buyer selects new shipping options and when they change shipping options. We recommend merchants subscribe to this if they want to be notified or need to recalculate amounts with\n        their callback URL when a selected shipping option changes for the current address. If SHIPPING_OPTIONS is not needed by the merchant, they should subscribe to SHIPPING_ADDRESS .\n\n \n\n### Configuring shipping preferences\nThe shipping preference is set using the payment_source.*.experience_context.shipping_preference field. There are 3 possible values:\n\n- GET_FROM_FILE : This default preference retrieves the customer-provided shipping address from their wallet.\n- NO_SHIPPING : This option removes the shipping address information from the review page and the API response. However, the shipping.phone_number and shipping.email_address fields are returned\n        for digital goods delivery.\n- SET_PROVIDED_ADDRESS : The review page shows the shipping address provided by the merchant in the create order request. The buyer cannot change this address on the review page. If the merchant does not pass an address, the\n        buyer can choose the address on the review page.\n\nIf you do not pass a shipping preference, the default behavior is GET_FROM_FILE . The review page shows the default shipping address from the buyer's wallet. The buyer can select a different shipping address from\n    their wallet or add a new address. Callbacks happen if the shipping preference is GET_FROM_FILE .\n\n\n### Passing a shipping address\nIf you have a shipping address from the buyer, pass it to Pay with PayPal or Pay with Venmoon the create order request. If you pass a shipping address with a shipping preference of GET_FROM_FILE , it will display on the review page, where the buyer can change the shipping address. You can use the shipping preference SET_PROVIDED_ADDRESS to prevent the buyer from changing the shipping address on the review page.   If your transaction does not involve shipping, you can pass the shipping preference NO_SHIPPING and no shipping information will be displayed on the review page.\n\nHere is a sample Create Order API request to a merchant with a callback config for Pay with PayPal ( payment_source:paypal ) and Pay with Venmo ( payment_source:venmo ).\n\n\n#### **`Pay with PayPal`**\n```curl\ncurl -v -X POST orders and includes selected addresses and options outside of the order object.\n\n\n\n- Sending order data is structurally similar to making a GET request.\n- Updated shipping addresses and options separately sent from the order to avoid confusion.\n- If the address or option is incomplete, it will not be set in order to prevent misunderstandings.\n- The cart identifier will be embedded in the callback URL if merchants cannot associate their shopping cart with the order.\n- Merchants with client-side shopping carts should include item details when they create the order for server-side shipping callbacks.\n\n \n\n### Callback request to merchant for shipping address event\nThe following sample is a server-side callback request to the merchant for a shipping event. The callback identifies the order, shipping_address , shipping_option and purchase_units .\n\n\n**warning**\nThe initial callback to the merchant does not include the \"shipping_option\" section.\n\n\n\n#### **`Sample - Callback request to merchant for shipping address event`**\n```javascript\n{\n  \"id\": \"5O190127TN364715T\",\n  \"shipping_address\": {\n    \"country_code\": \"US\",\n    \"admin_area_1\": \"TX\",\n    \"admin_area_2\": \"Dallas\",\n    \"postal_code\": \"75001\"\n  },\n  \"shipping_option\": {\n    \"id\": \"2\",\n    \"amount\": {\n      \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n      \"value\": \"20.00\"\n    },\n    \"type\": \"SHIPPING\",\n    \"label\": \"Free Shipping\"\n  },\n  \"purchase_units\": [{\n    \"reference_id\": \"d9f80740-38f0-11e8-b467-0ed5f89f718b\",\n    \"amount\": {\n      \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n      \"value\": \"100.00\"\n    }\n  }]\n}\n```\n\n### Callback request fields\n| **Field** | **Description** | **Data type** |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| id | Unique identifier for the shipping order. For example, 5O190127TN364715T . | string |\n| shipping_address | Shipping address information. Includes country_code , admin_area_1 , admin_area_2 , and postal_code . | object |\n| country_code | Identifies the shipping address country. For example, US . | string |\n| admin_area_1 | Identifies the shipping address state or region. For example, TX . | string |\n| admin_area_2 | Identifies the shipping address, city, or municipality. For example, Dallas . | string |\n| postal_code | Identifies the postal code. For example, 7500 . | number |\n| shipping_option | Shipping option information. Includes id , amount , type , label , and selected . | string |\n| selected | Determines which option is selected by default.Possible values aretrueorfalse | boolean |\n| id | Indicates the type of shipping option. For example, 2 . | number |\n| amount | Shipping option amount. Includes currency_code and value . | object |\n| currency_code | Indicates the type of currency. For example, USD . | string |\n| value | String denoting the purchase price and shipping option price, formatted as X.XX . For example, 2.00 . | number |\n| type | An enum that indicates the type of shipping. For example, SHIPPING or PICKUP . | string |\n| label | Dropdown menu option selected by the buyer. Indicates whether the shipping is free or not. For example, Free Shipping . | string |\n| purchase_units | Defines the purchase unit. Includes reference_id and amount . | object |\n| reference_id | Identifier associated with the purchase units. For example, d9f80740-38f0-11e8-b467-0ed5f89f718b . | string |\n\n\nThe merchant response to a server-side callback request is similar to an order. A change to the customers shipping address or options can affect the following fields within the data structure:\n\n\n\n- purchase_units[].shipping.options represent the shipping modules associated with the purchase units within the order. The purchase order field includes contact and delivery information, including phone\n        number,account email address, order ID, and reference ID.\n- purchase_units[].amount represents the purchase unit amount in the order.\n\nBuyer changes can be managed throughone of the following approaches:\n\n\n\n- Asking the merchant to return an updated order limited to the fields that can be changed.\n- Asking the merchant to return a list of patch operations.\n\n \n\n### Merchant success response\nWhen the order request is acceptable, the merchant responds with a success message that contains amount and shipping option changes.\n\nHere is a sample HTTP 200 OK callback response from a merchant with shipping options and amount updates.\n\n\n#### **`Code sample, Merchant success response`**\n```javascript\n{\n  \"id\": \"8HFTASDATTV\",\n  \"purchase_units\": [{\n    \"reference_id\": \"d9f80740-38f0-11e8-b467-0ed5f89f718b\",\n    \"amount\": {\n      \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n      \"value\": \"105.00\",\n      \"breakdown\": {\n        \"item_total\": {\n          \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n          \"value\": \"100.00\"\n        },\n        \"tax_total\": {\n          \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n          \"value\": \"5.00\"\n        },\n        \"shipping\": {\n          \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n          \"value\": \"0.00\"\n        }\n      }\n    },\n    \"shipping_options\": [{\n      \"id\": \"1\",\n      \"amount\": {\n        \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n        \"value\": \"0.00\"\n      },\n      \"type\": \"SHIPPING\",\n      \"label\": \"Free Shipping\",\n      \"selected\": true\n    }, {\n      \"id\": \"2\",\n      \"amount\": {\n        \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n        \"value\": \"7.00\"\n      },\n      \"type\": \"SHIPPING\",\n      \"label\": \"USPS Priority Shipping\",\n      \"selected\": false\n    }, {\n      \"id\": \"3\",\n      \"amount\": {\n        \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n        \"value\": \"10.00\"\n      },\n      \"type\": \"SHIPPING\",\n      \"label\": \"1-Day Shipping\",\n      \"selected\": false\n    }]\n  }]\n}\n```\n\n### Merchant success response fields\nA merchant response can include the fields identified in the following table.\n\n| **Field** | **Description** | **Date type** |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| id | Identifies the merchant. For example, 8HFTASDATTV . | string |\n| purchase_units | Purchase unit information. Includes reference_id and amount . | object |\n| reference_id | Uniquely identifies the purchase transaction. For example, d9f80740-38f0-11e8-b467-0ed5f89f718b . | string |\n| amount | Purchase unit amount in the order. Includes currency_code , value , and breakdown . | object |\n| currency_code | Code indicating the amount currency type. For example, USD . | string |\n| value | String denoting the purchase unit amount in the order, formatted as X.XX . For example, 105.00 . | amount |\n| breakdown | Amount breakdown. Includes item_total , tax_total, and shipping . | object |\n| item_total | Amount item breakdown. Includes currency_code and value . | object |\n| value | Amount item value. For example, 100.0 . | number |\n| tax_total | Amount tax breakdown. Includes currency_code and value . | object |\n| value | String denoting the tax_total amount, formatted as X.XX . For example, 5.00 . | number |\n| shipping | Amount shipping breakdown. Includes currency_code and value . | object |\n| value | String denoting the value. amount, formatted as X.XX . For example, 0.00 .\n\nIn this example, there are no shipping costs associated with the purchase unit. | number |\n| shipping_options | Shipping option information. Includes id , amount , type , label , and selected . | object |\n| selected | Determines which options are selected by default. Possible values aretrueorfalse. | boolean |\n| id | Shipping option identifier. For example, 1 . | number |\n| amount | Amount for the selected shipping option. For example, currency_code and value . | object |\n| value | String denoting the value. amount for the selected shipping option, formatted as X.XX . For example, 0.00 . The value depends upon the selected label . | number |\n| type | An enum that indicates the type of delivery for the selected option. For example, SHIPPING or PICKUP . | string |\n| label | Dropdown menu option selected by the buyer. Indicates the type of SHIPPING . For example, Free Shipping .   Other labels include USPS Priority Shipping and 1-Day Shipping . | string |\n\nThe order amount automatically updates based on the options selected by buyers unless you are subscribed to the shipping_options callback. If you are subscribed to shipping_options , ensure the callback response includes the updated total cost so that the checkout page can be updated.You can use the onShippingOptionsChange() callback to update your own database with the new cost amount.\n\n\n### Merchant decline response\nA merchant can issue a 422 error to decline a callback event.In the response, the merchant should provide a reason why the callback is being declined. The following reasons are supported:\n\n| Callback event type | Error | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| Shipping address | ADDRESS_ERROR | Your order can't be shipped to this address. |\n| Shipping address | COUNTRY_ERROR | Your order can't be shipped to this country. |\n| Shipping address | STATE_ERROR | Your order can't be shipped to this state. |\n| Shipping address | ZIP_ERROR | Your order can't be shipped to this zip. |\n| Shipping option | METHOD_UNAVAILABLE | The shipping method you selected is unavailable. To continue, choose another way to get your order. |\n| Shipping option | STORE_UNAVAILABLE | Part of your order isn't available at this store. |\n\n \n\nHere is a sample decline callback from the merchant. In this case, there is an HTTP 422 Unprocessable Entity response, which is a country error.\n\n\n#### **`Code sample, Decline callback`**\n```javascript\n{\n  \"name\": \"UNPROCESSABLE_ENTITY\",\n  \"details\": [{\n    \"issue\": \"COUNTRY_ERROR\"\n  }]\n}\n```\n"},"routes/__docs-pages":null},"actionData":null,"errors":null},"future":{"v2_dev":true,"unstable_postcss":false,"unstable_tailwind":false,"v2_errorBoundary":false,"v2_headers":false,"v2_meta":true,"v2_normalizeFormMethod":true,"v2_routeConvention":false}};</script><script nonce="Asyk0V1wUNPw45lUTIRyx+K/8XMHskx5yKCJ7PMHNBDqmm8Y" type="module" async="">import "https://www.paypalobjects.com/ppdevdocs/bundles/10.6.8/manifest-2AA28ED2.js";

for(var key in bannerFptiData){ closebannerFptiData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; fptiRecordClick(closebannerFptiData); }; } if (acceptAllButton && cookieBanner && cookieLanguage) { acceptAllButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(true , cookieObjSetup('close')); }; } window.hideGdprBanner = function () { var cookieBannerUi = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if (cookieBannerUi && cookieBannerUi.className.indexOf('ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile') === -1) { cookieBannerUi.className += " ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile"; } }; window.showGdprBanner = function () { var cookieBannerUi = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if (cookieBannerUi) { cookieBannerUi.className = cookieBannerUi.className.replace("ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile",""); } }; document.body.addEventListener("focus", function (event) { if (event.target.type === 'text' || event.target.type === 'number' || event.target.type === 'password' || event.target.type === 'email' || event.target.type === 'select-one') { window.hideGdprBanner(); } }, true); } function adjustPaddingTop(){ var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll.length > 0){ var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); var bannerHeight = cookieBanner ? cookieBanner.clientHeight : 0; if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0] && bannerHeight){ cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingTop = bannerHeight/16 +'em'; } } }; var isPaddingBottomAdded = false, bannerPaddingBottom = ""; function adjustPaddingBottom(addListener){ if (undefined || !false) { return; } function adjustPaddingBottomEvent() { var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll.length > 0){ var bodyPaddingBottom = cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom; var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0] && cookieBanner.style.display != 'none') { if (bodyPaddingBottom === "" || (isPaddingBottomAdded && bannerPaddingBottom === bodyPaddingBottom)) { var cookieBannerContainer = document.getElementsByClassName('ccpaCookieBanner_container'); var bannerBottomHeight = cookieBannerContainer.length > 0 ? parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(cookieBannerContainer[0]).bottom.replace("px", "")) : 0; var bannerHeight = cookieBanner ? cookieBanner.clientHeight : 0; bannerPaddingBottom = ((bannerHeight + bannerBottomHeight) / 16) + 'em'; cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom = bannerPaddingBottom; isPaddingBottomAdded = true; } else if (isPaddingBottomAdded && bannerPaddingBottom !== bodyPaddingBottom) { isPaddingBottomAdded = false; } } } } if (addListener) { adjustPaddingBottomEvent(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingBottomEvent);  } else { var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0]){ window.removeEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingBottomEvent); adjustPaddingBottomEvent(); if (isPaddingBottomAdded && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom === bannerPaddingBottom) { cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.removeProperty('padding-bottom'); } } } }; window.bindGdprEvents = bindGdprEvents; function cookieDisabled() { if (navigator.cookieEnabled === false) return "true"; else if (navigator.cookieEnabled === true) return "false"; else return "undefined"; }; function fptiLogActivity(winFptiData){ window.PAYPAL.analytics.Analytics.prototype.logActivity({...winFptiData, product:"cookieBanner"}); }; function gdprSetup () { var cookieLanguage = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieContent_wrapper'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); var manageLink = document.getElementById('manageCookiesLink'); var acceptAllLink = document.getElementById('acceptAllButton'); var trackingPageName = '' || getFptiPage() || document.title;    } } var pageName = trackingPageName || getFptiPage() || document.title; var winFptiData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify((window && window.fpti) || {})); if(false){ bannerFptiData.isNativeBannerHidden = true; } for(var key in bannerFptiData){ winFptiData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; winFptiData['event_name'] = 'cookie_banner_shown'; fptiLogActivity(winFptiData); if (manageLink) { manageLink.setAttribute('pagename', (pageName + '|managecookies')); } if (acceptAllLink) { acceptAllLink.setAttribute('pagename', (pageName + '|acceptcookies')); } bindGdprEvents(); }; function hideBanner() { var cookieLanguage = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieContent_wrapper'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if(cookieLanguage && cookieBanner){ cookieLanguage.style.display = 'none'; cookieBanner.style.display = 'none'; }else { return false; } window.removeEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop); var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0]){ cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.removeProperty('padding-top'); } document.body.className = document.body.className.replace("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll",""); document.body.className = document.body.className.replace("top-cookie-banner-enabled",""); return true; } function isPageReady () { var cookieBannerUi = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); return !!(cookieBannerUi && getFptiReqData()); } function enableFocusEvent(addListener){ if(!false || undefined){ return; } var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); function focusIn(e) { if(cookieBanner && cookieBanner.style.display != 'none'){ var activeElement = document.activeElement; if(((activeElement.getBoundingClientRect().bottom) > (cookieBanner.getBoundingClientRect().top)) && !activeElement.parentElement.nodeName.includes("UL")){ activeElement.scrollIntoView({block: 'center'}); } }else{ document.removeEventListener("focusin", focusIn); } } if(addListener){ document.addEventListener("focusin",focusIn); } } function enableEvents(enable){ adjustPaddingBottom(enable); enableFocusEvent(enable); } var maxRetries = 34, bannerhidden=false; function triggerBanner() { if (isPageReady()) { cookieFiltering('pageLoad'); if(true){setTimeout(function(){ cookieFiltering('afterPageLoad')}, 3000);} if (isBannerClosed()) { hideBanner(); } if(false){ setSessionStorage('isInvisibleBanner'); } gdprSetup(); } else { if (isBannerClosed() && !bannerhidden ) { bannerhidden=hideBanner(); } if (maxRetries-- > 0) { setTimeout(triggerBanner, 150); } else { cookieFiltering('pageLoad'); if(true){setTimeout(function(){ cookieFiltering('afterPageLoad')}, 3000);} if (isBannerClosed()) { hideBanner(); } if(!isBannerClosed() && document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner') && !document.body.className.includes("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll")){ document.body.className = document.body.className += " ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"; if(undefined){ adjustPaddingTop(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop);   document.body.className = document.body.className += " top-cookie-banner-enabled"; } } var acceptAllButton = document.getElementById('acceptAllButton'); var bannerDeclineButton = document.getElementById('bannerDeclineButton'); var bannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('bannerCloseButton'); var usBannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('usBannerCloseButton'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if ( acceptAllButton ) { acceptAllButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('accept')); }; } if ( bannerDeclineButton ) { bannerDeclineButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('decline')); }; } if ( usBannerCloseButton ) { usBannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('close')); }; } if ( bannerCloseButton ) { bannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); setSessionStorage('isBannerClosed'); } } if(false){ setSessionStorage('isInvisibleBanner'); } } } } triggerBanner(); })();</script></div></body></html>
